*The Klingon Way* in {pIqaD}
============================
Here, presented in <nobr><img src="piq/sml/p.gif" width="11" height="19"
alt="p"><img src="piq/sml/i.gif" width="14" height="19"
alt="I"><img src="piq/sml/q.gif" width="8" height="19"
alt="q"><img src="piq/sml/a.gif" width="14" height="19"
alt="a"><img src="piq/sml/d.gif" width="12" height="19" alt="D">,</nobr> are
the 160 Klingon sayings discussed in the book <I>The Klingon Way</I> (by Marc
Okrand). For further information as to their meanings and usage, page
references to that book has been included.
